          <div style="width:52px">
           <a href="/wiki/File:Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg" class="image"><img alt="Crystal Clear app kedit.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg/40px-Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg/60px-Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg/80px-Crystal_Clear_app_kedit.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128"></a>
          </div></td>
         <td class="mbox-text">
          <div class="mbox-text-span">
           This section may need to be <b>rewritten</b> to comply with Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style">quality standards</a>, as this in part reads like an advertisement but the English requires clean-up for readability.<span class="hide-when-compact"> <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Republic_of_the_Congo&amp;action=edit">You can help</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Talk:Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Talk:Republic of the Congo">talk page</a> may contain suggestions.</span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">April 2020</span>)</i></small>
          </div></td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <p>Congolese singers have become known internationally: the Franco-Congolese rapper <a href="/wiki/Passi" title="Passi">Passi</a>'s work is broadcast in France, and he has released several hit albums, such as <i>Temptations</i>, with the famous song "I zap and I mate." Other notable musicians include <a href="/w/index.php?title=M%27Passi&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="M'Passi (page does not exist)">M'Passi</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%27Passi" class="extiw" title="fr:M'Passi">fr</a>]</span>, singer of the former group <a href="/w/index.php?title=Melgroove&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Melgroove (page does not exist)">Melgroove</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Melgroove" class="extiw" title="fr:Melgroove">fr</a>]</span>; rappers <a href="/wiki/Calbo_(rapper)" title="Calbo (rapper)">Calbo</a> of <a href="/wiki/%C3%84rsenik" title="Ärsenik">Ärsenik</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ben_J" class="mw-redirect" title="Ben J">Ben J</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ben_J" class="extiw" title="fr:Ben J">fr</a>]</span> of <a href="/wiki/N%C3%A8g%27_Marrons" class="mw-redirect" title="Nèg' Marrons">Nèg' Marrons</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/N%C3%A8g%27_Marrons" class="extiw" title="fr:Nèg' Marrons">fr</a>]</span>, Mystic, RCFA, the group <a href="/wiki/Bisso_Na_Bisso" title="Bisso Na Bisso">Bisso Na Bisso</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Casimir_Zao&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Casimir Zao (page does not exist)">Casimir Zao</a><span class="noprint" style="font-size:85%; font-style: normal;">&nbsp;[<a href="https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zao_(chanteur)" class="extiw" title="fr:Zao (chanteur)">fr</a>]</span>. </p>
      <p>Several writers from the Republic of Congo have become recognised elsewhere in Africa and the French-speaking world, including <a href="/wiki/Alain_Mabanckou" title="Alain Mabanckou">Alain Mabanckou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jean-Baptiste_Tati_Loutard" title="Jean-Baptiste Tati Loutard">Jean-Baptiste Tati Loutard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jeannette_Balou_Tchichelle" title="Jeannette Balou Tchichelle">Jeannette Balou Tchichelle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Henri_Lopes" class="mw-redirect" title="Henri Lopes">Henri Lopes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lassy_Mbouity" title="Lassy Mbouity">Lassy Mbouity</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Tchicaya_U_Tam%27si" title="Tchicaya U Tam'si">Tchicaya U Tam'si</a>. </p>
      <p>Artists have struggled to build a film industry. After a promising start in the 1970s, the troubled political situation closed cinemas and made film production difficult. Instead of making feature films for distribution to theaters, filmmakers generally directly stream their video productions on the internet. </p>
      <p>Congolese culture, art, and media have suffered from a lack of investment due to the unstable political conditions and warfare. </p> 
      <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Republic_of_the_Congo&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Main article: <a href="/wiki/Education_in_the_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Education in the Republic of the Congo">Education in the Republic of the Congo</a>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg/220px-SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg/330px-SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b6/SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg/440px-SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="784" data-file-height="588"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:SAINTE_RITA_CONG-BR2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>School children in the classroom, Republic of the Congo
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>Public expenditure of the GDP was less in 2002–05 than in 1991.<sup id="cite_ref-hdrstats.undp.org_73-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hdrstats.undp.org-73">[73]</a></sup> Public education is theoretically free and mandatory for under-16-year-olds<sup id="cite_ref-unhcr.org_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unhcr.org-78">[78]</a></sup> but, in practice, expenses exist.<sup id="cite_ref-unhcr.org_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unhcr.org-78">[78]</a></sup> In 2005 net primary enrollment rate was 44%, a significant drop from the 79% in 1991.<sup id="cite_ref-hdrstats.undp.org_73-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hdrstats.undp.org-73">[73]</a></sup> Education between ages six and sixteen is compulsory. Pupils who complete six years of primary school and seven years of secondary school obtain a baccalaureate. </p>
      <p>The country has universities where students can obtain a bachelor's degree in three years and a master's in five. <a href="/wiki/Marien_Ngouabi_University" title="Marien Ngouabi University">Marien Ngouabi University</a>—which offers courses in medicine, law, and other fields—is the country's only public university. </p>
      <p>Instruction at all levels is in <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>, and the educational system as a whole models the French system. </p>

         <li id="cite_note-48"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-48">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"> With inconsistent figures: 
           <ul>
            <li>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.presidence.cg/congo/administration.php">site of the Presidency of the Republic of the Congo</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090727221905/http://www.presidence.cg/congo/administration.php">Archived</a> 27 July 2009 at the <a href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">Wayback Machine</a> lists 11 departments, 7 communes, and 76 districts.</li> 
            <li>The 2004 <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.cnsee.org/Publication/Annuaire_04.pdf">Statistical directory of Congo</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20091113142137/http://www.cnsee.org/Publication/Annuaire_04.pdf">Archived</a> 13 November 2009 at the <a href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">Wayback Machine</a> lists 12 departments, 6 communes, and 85 districts</li> 
            <li>A list of subprefects (higher representatives of State in a district) nominated in December 2008 lists 86 districts. Search 
             <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"><cite class="citation web cs1"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090116112954/http://www.zenga-mambu.com/fiche.php?id=693">"Archived copy"</a>. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">6 August</span> 2009</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Archived+copy&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.zenga-mambu.com%2Ffiche.php%3Fid%3D693&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ARepublic+of+the+Congo" class="Z3988"></span><span class="cs1-maint citation-comment">CS1 maint: archived copy as title (<a href="/wiki/Category:CS1_maint:_archived_copy_as_title" title="Category:CS1 maint: archived copy as title">link</a>)</span></li> 
            <li>Finally, the good figures seem to come from <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.congo-siteportail.info/Les-donnees-generales-sur-le-Congo_a18.html">this site</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20090518092837/http://www.congo-siteportail.info/Les-donnees-generales-sur-le-Congo_a18.html">Archived</a> 18 May 2009 at the <a href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">Wayback Machine</a>: 12 departments, 7 communes, and 86 districts</li>
           </ul> </span></li>
